msg:We originally planned to take advantage of the New Year to soak in the hot springs here and then go to Mount Lushan for fun. Who knew that this would happen the next morning? I will never come to Tianmu Hot Spring Resort Hotel again.
My sister was beaten up at Tianmu Hot Spring Hotel because of a car incident. . .
You have to take a car to eat at this hotel. When the car came, my sister, my two daughters and I were ready to get on. There were three seats in a row. My eldest daughter and my sister had already got on. A woman in white clothes squeezed the door of the car to prevent my aunt and my mother from getting on. Then we couldn't argue, so my aunt asked my sister to get off the car, saying "We will get off and not sit anymore." She was going to wait for the car behind with my aunt, but who knew that the woman was still blocking the door of the car. My sister said, "I asked you to sit, but you won't let me get off?" The woman got angry for no reason, and she and her relatives, a total of five people, grabbed my sister and beat her. My family members are all women, and my aunt, my mother, and my eldest aunt went up to protect my sister. When she was beaten, no security personnel of the hotel stepped forward to stop it. The front desk was watching the show on the side. I was the first to call the police. A staff member came to persuade the fight, but the other party didn't listen at all and still rushed up to beat me. In the end, the hotel shirked all responsibilities. I want to ask: 1. Why is there no security personnel in the hotel? 2. There were many people at the hotel lobby entrance during breakfast time, why were there no staff to maintain order? 3. Why didn't they call the police immediately when provoking a quarrel, but instead stood by and watched? 4. Later, the police intervened and asked to retrieve the personnel information, but the hotel did not cooperate. The check-in registration information could not be found (the reason was that the platform could not see the information when registering, and then said that the guest could not find it when checking out). Would eight people check in without identity information registration? The phone number left was still an empty number
For a hotel with no security, where can't you get safety protection when something happens, where do the good reviews on the Internet come from?
Hygiene: Poor
Environment: Poor
Service: Very poor attitude
Facilities: Poor
